Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-12 Property owners failing to appear at hearings -- Waiver of rights.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Every person who has real property within the boundaries of the district and who fails to appear before the governing body at the hearing and make any objection he may have to the creation of the district, the making of the improvements and the inclusion of his real property in the district, shall be deemed to have waived every such objection. Such waiver shall not, however, preclude his right to object to the amount of the assessment at the hearing for which provision is made in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-13 Assessment list to be prepared.
-------------------------------------------------------------
After a decision is taken by a governing body to proceed with the district and project, it shall cause to be prepared an assessment list detailing the total amount to be assessed, the specific properties assessed, and the amount of assessment on each piece of property.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-14 Declaration of costs -- Contents of resolution.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
After the preparation of the proposed assessment list, the governing body shall cause to be prepared for adoption at the hearing hereinafter provided for, a resolution declaring the entire cost of the improvement including the cost of construction as determined from the costs and feasibility report and other incidental costs, legal and fiscal fees and costs, the cost of the publication of notices and all other costs properly incident to the construction of the improvement and the financing thereof. Such resolution shall specify what share, if any, of the total cost is payable from sources other than the imposition of assessments and shall incorporate the proposed assessment list provided for in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-15 Board of equalization and review -- Appointment -- Functions and authority.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Whenever the governing body of any municipality shall propose to levy any tax under any provision of this chapter, it shall before doing so, appoint a board of equalization and review which shall consist of three or more of its members.  This board shall perform the functions of the governing body under Sections

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-16 Notice of assessment -- Publication.
------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-16(1): 54-8-14 After the preparation of a resolution under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-16(2): (1); 63G-30-102; 63G-30-102(3)
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-16(2)(a): (1); 63G-30-102 The governing body shall provide the notice described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-16(2)(b): 63G-30-102(3) The addresses to be used for the purpose of mailing notice as required by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-16(2)(b)(i): the last address appearing on the real property assessment rolls of the county for each owner of real property whose property will be assessed for part of the cost of the improvement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-16(2)(b)(ii): the street number of each piece of improved property to be affected by the proposed assessment.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-16(3): Each notice shall state that at the specified time and place, the governing body will hold a public hearing upon the proposed assessments and shall state that any owner of any property to be assessed pursuant to the resolution will be heard on the question of whether the owner's property will be benefited by the proposed improvement to the amount of the proposed assessment against the owner's property and whether the amount assessed against the owner's property constitutes more than the owner's proper proportional share of the total cost of the improvement.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-17 Assessments -- Hearings on -- Corrections of -- Assessment not to exceed benefit.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
On the date and at the time and place specified in the aforesaid notice, the governing body shall, in open and public session, hear all arguments relating to the benefits accruing to any tract, block, lot or parcel of land therein and the amounts proposed to be assessed against any such tract, block, lot or parcel. The hearing may be adjourned from time to time to a fixed future time and place. After the hearing has been concluded and all persons desiring to be heard have been heard, the governing body shall consider the arguments presented and shall make such corrections in the assessment list as may be considered just and equitable. Such corrections may eliminate, may increase, or may decrease the amount of the assessment proposed to be levied against any piece of property. However, no increase of any proposed assessment shall be valid unless the owner of the property is given notice and an opportunity to be heard. After such corrections have been made, the governing body shall make a specific finding that no proposed assessment on the corrected assessment list exceeds the benefit to be derived from the improvement by the piece of property to be so assessed and that no piece of property so listed will bear more than its proper proportionate share of the cost of such improvement.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-18 Assessments -- Resolution to adopt.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
After the public hearing has been concluded and all corrections made to the assessment list, and in the case of a municipality, after receiving the report from the board of equalization and review, the governing body shall proceed to adopt the assessment resolution.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19 Assessments -- Right to levy against property -- Due date -- Notice -- Payment in annual installments.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(1): The governing body may levy the assessments under the assessment list in whole or in part at any time after the adoption of the assessment resolution, but if not levied as a whole, any partial levies shall be made on the basis of completed improvements and the property benefited by the improvements.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(2): The amount of the assessment will become due and collectible immediately upon the levying of the assessment and, if it is not paid within 30 days from the date of the levy, it shall, at the expiration of the 30 days, commence to bear interest at a rate fixed by the governing body but not to exceed 7% per annum.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(3): 54-8-16; (3)(a); 54-8-26(2)
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(3)(a): 54-8-16 Notice shall be given in the same manner as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(3)(b): (3)(a); 54-8-26(2) The notice under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(3)(b)(i): specify the date and amount of the levy affecting each tract, block, lot, or parcel, the date when interest will commence, the amount of such interest, and the period of years over which installment payments may be made;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(3)(b)(ii): 54-8-26(2) identify the easement that may be acquired by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(3)(b)(iii): be recorded in the office of the recorder of the county in which the tract, block, lot, or parcel is located.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(4)(a): If the assessment is not paid within the 30 days allowed, each owner shall be presumed to exercise the right and option to pay the amount due in equal annual installments bearing interest at the rate specified in the notice and extending over the period of years, not exceeding 20 specified in the notice.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(4)(b): The first installment shall become due one year from the date when interest commenced, and one installment shall become due on the same day of the same month annually thereafter.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-19(4)(c): Any assessment may be prepaid on any annual installment date without interest penalty provided the total balance of the assessment, including accrued interest, costs and penalties, be paid.


Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-20 Assessments -- Failure to pay installment -- Interest and penalties -- Lien on property -- Sale of property -- Disposition of proceeds.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The failure to pay any installment and any interest thereon when due shall ipso facto cause all other installments and the interest thereon to become due and payable and the governing body shall, within 30 days from the date of such default, proceed against the property for the collection of the total amount due thereon, including interest plus 10% additional on unpaid principal and interest as penalties and costs of collection. Special assessments levied hereunder shall rank on an equality with taxes levied against the property assessed by the state, the county and all other taxing districts, and no sale of property for the nonpayment of taxes or other special assessments shall extinguish the lien of other than the taxes or special assessments for the nonpayment of which such sale is had. The proceeds of the sale of any property for nonpayment of special assessments shall be applied in the discharge of such assessments, the interest thereon, costs and penalties. If there are outstanding any special improvement bonds issued pursuant to the improvement in question, proceeds of the sale of any property for nonpayment of any special assessments shall after the payment therefrom of the costs of collection be applied to the costs of redemption prior to maturity of as many of the outstanding special improvement bonds as can be retired with the amount available. Any surplus remaining after the payment of amounts due shall be paid over to the owner of the property sold. The lien of special assessments levied hereunder shall be superior to all other liens against the property assessed except that it shall be on a parity with the lien of ad valorem taxes and a lien of other special assessments and shall be effective from and after the date upon which the resolution levying the assessments is adopted.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-21 Assessments -- Prepayment of unpaid installments.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The governing body may in the resolution levying the assessments provide that all unpaid installments of assessments levied against any piece of property may (but only in their entirety) be paid prior to the dates on which they become due if the property owner paying such installments pays all interest which would accrue thereon to the next succeeding date on which interest is payable on the bonds issued in anticipation of the collection of the assessments, together with such additional amount of interest as in the opinion of the governing body is necessary to assure the availability of money fully sufficient to pay interest on the bonds as interest becomes due and any redemption premiums which may become payable on the bonds in order to retire in advance of maturity bonds in a sufficient amount to utilize the assessments thus paid in advance. If no bonds have been issued then all unpaid installments of assessments levied against any piece of property may be paid in their entirety prior to the date upon which they become due by paying the principal amount due and the interest accrued thereon to the date of payment.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-22 Bonds -- Issuance authorized -- Amount -- Interest -- Additional requirements.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
After the expiration of 30 days from the date of the adoption of the resolution levying the assessments, the county legislative body may issue negotiable interest-bearing bonds in a principal amount not exceeding the unpaid balance of the assessments levied.  The bonds shall bear interest at not exceeding 7% per annum, payable semiannually or annually, and shall mature serially over a period not exceeding 20 years, but in no event shall such bonds extend over a longer period of time than the period of time over which such installments of special assessments are due and payable and 90 days thereafter.  The bonds shall be of such form and denomination and shall be payable in principal and interest at such times and place, and shall be sold, authorized, and issued in such manner as the county legislative body may determine.  The bonds shall be dated no earlier than the date on which the special assessment shall begin to bear interest, and shall be secured by and payable from the irrevocable pledge and dedication of the funds derived from the levy and collection of the special assessments in anticipation of the collection of which they are issued.  Any premium received on the sale of the bonds may be applied as other bond proceeds or if not so applied the same shall be placed in the fund for the payment of principal of and interest on the bonds.  The bonds shall be callable for redemption from the proceeds of any property sold for the nonpayment of special assessments but not otherwise unless the bonds on the face thereof provide for redemption prior to maturity, and the county legislative body may provide that the bonds shall be redeemable on any interest payment date or dates prior to maturity pursuant to such notice and at such premiums as it deems advisable.  The bonds shall be signed by the county executive and the chair of the county legislative body and shall be countersigned by the city recorder or the clerk of the board of the town trustees or the clerk of the county legislative body, whichever is applicable, and one of such signatures may be a facsimile signature.  Interest may be evidenced by interest coupons attached to such bonds and signed by a facsimile signature of one of the individuals who signed the bond.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-23 Objection to amount of assessment -- Civil action -- Litigation to question or attack proceedings or legality of bonds -- Notice.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-23(1): No special assessment levied under this chapter shall be declared void, nor shall any such assessment or part thereof be set aside in consequence of any error or irregularity permitted or appearing in any of the proceedings under this chapter, but any party feeling aggrieved by any such special assessment or proceeding may bring a civil action to cause such grievance to be adjudicated if such action is commenced prior to the expiration of the period specified in this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-23(2): The burden of proof to show that such special assessment or part thereof is invalid, inequitable or unjust shall rest upon the party who brings such suit.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-23(3): 54-8-18 Any such litigation shall not be regarded as an appeal within the meaning of the prohibition contained in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-23(5): For a period of 20 days after the governing body has adopted the enactment authorizing the assessment, any taxpayer in the district shall have the right to institute litigation for the purpose of questioning or attacking the proceedings pursuant to which the assessments have been authorized subject to the provisions of the preceding paragraph.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-23(7): For a period of 20 days thereafter, any person whose property shall have been assessed and any taxpayer in the district shall have the right to institute litigation for the purpose of questioning or attacking the legality of such bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-23(8): After the expiration of such 20-day period, all proceedings theretofore had by the governing body, the bonds to be issued pursuant thereto, and the special assessments from which such bonds are to be paid, shall become incontestable, and no suit attacking or questioning the legality thereof may be instituted in this state, and no court shall have the authority to inquire into such matters.

----------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-28 Additional overhead facilities prohibited -- Exception.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Once removed, no overhead electric or communication facilities shall be installed within the boundary of a local improvement district for conversion of overhead electric and communication facilities in nominal voltages of less than 35,000 volts.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-29 Jurisdiction over public utilities.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Nothing contained in this chapter shall vest any jurisdiction over public utilities in the governing bodies. The Public Service Commission of Utah shall retain all jurisdiction now or hereafter conferred upon it by law.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8-30 Commencement of conversion -- When required.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
If an improvement district is established pursuant to this chapter, the public utility corporations involved shall not be required to commence conversion until the ordinance, the assessment roll and issuance of bonds have become final and no civil action has been filed or if civil action has been filed, until the decision of the court upon the action has become final and is not subject to further appeal.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 54 - Chapter 8a - Damage to Underground Utility Facilities
**************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2 Definitions.
------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(1): 54-8a-9 "Association" means two or more operators organized to receive notification of excavation activities in a specified area, as provided by Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(2): 54-8a-13 "Board" means the Underground Facilities Damage Dispute Board created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(3): "Emergency" means an occurrence or suspected natural gas leak necessitating immediate action to prevent or mitigate loss of, or damage to, life, health, property, or essential public services.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(4): "Excavate" or "excavation" means an operation in which earth, rock, or other material on or below the ground is moved or displaced by tools, equipment, or explosives.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(5): "Excavator" means any person or entity that excavates or conducts excavation activities.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(6): "48 hours" means a 48-hour period occurring during business days which includes any day except Saturday, Sunday, or a legal holiday.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(7): "Hand tool" means an implement:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(7)(a): powered by hand; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(7)(b): designed to avoid damaging an underground facility, including a vacuum excavation tool and air knife.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(8): 54-8a-4(3); 54-8a-5(2)(b)(ii) "Location" means the site of a proposed area of excavation described:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(8)(a): 54-8a-4(3); 54-8a-5(2)(b)(ii)
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(8)(a)(i): by street address, if available;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(8)(a)(ii): by the area at that street address to be excavated; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(8)(a)(iii): 54-8a-4(3); 54-8a-5(2)(b)(ii) as specified in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(8)(b): if there is no street address available, by the area of excavation using any available designations, including a nearby street or road, an intersection, GPS coordinates, or other generally accepted methods.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(9): "Location request assignment" means a number assigned to a proposed excavation by an association or operator upon receiving notice of the proposed excavation from the excavator.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(10): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(10)(a): "Operator" means a person who owns, operates, or maintains an underground facility.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(10)(b): "Operator" does not include an owner of real property where underground facilities are:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(10)(b)(i): located within:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(10)(b)(i)(A): the owner's property; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(10)(b)(i)(B): a public street adjacent to the owner's property, a right-of-way adjacent to the owner's property, or a public utility easement adjacent to the owner's property;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(10)(b)(ii): used exclusively to furnish services to the owner's property; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(10)(b)(iii): maintained under the operation and control of that owner.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(11): (11)(a) "Person" includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(11)(a): an individual, government entity, corporation, partnership, association, or company; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(11)(b): (11)(a) the trustee, receiver, assignee, and personal representative of a person listed in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(12): "Sewer lateral cleanout" means a point of access where a sewer lateral can be serviced.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(13): "24 hours" means a 24-hour period, excluding hours occurring during a Saturday, Sunday, or a legal holiday.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14): "Underground facility" means personal property that is buried or placed below ground level for use in the storage or conveyance of any of the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14)(a): water;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14)(b): sewage, including sewer laterals;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14)(c): communications, including electronic, photonic, telephonic, or telegraphic communications;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14)(d): television, cable television, or other telecommunication signals, including transmission to subscribers of video or other programming;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14)(e): electric power;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14)(f): oil, gas, or other fluid and gaseous substances;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14)(g): steam;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14)(h): slurry; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-2(14)(i): dangerous materials or products.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-3(1)(d): a statement concerning whether the operator is a member of an association and, if the operator is a member of an association, the name of and contact information for the association.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-3(2): In a county where an association is established, the association shall file its telephone number and a list of its members who are operators with the county clerk on behalf of any participating operator.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-5.5 Determining the precise location of marked underground facilities.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-5.5(1): 54-8a-5 An excavator may not use any power-operated or power-driven excavating or boring equipment within 24 inches of the markings made in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-5.5(1)(a): the excavator determines the exact location of the underground facility by excavating with hand tools to confirm that the excavation will not damage the underground facilities; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-5.5(1)(b): the operator provides an excavator with written or electronic notice waiving the requirement that the excavator determine the exact location of the underground facilities by excavating with hand tools.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-5.5(2): Power-operated or power-driven excavating or boring equipment may be used for the removal of any existing pavement if there is no underground facility contained in the pavement, as marked by the operator.


Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-5.8 Excavator access.
-------------------------------------------------
An excavator may enter or access an owner's property or dwelling to locate a sewer lateral with the owner's permission.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-7 Notice of damage -- Repairs.
----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-7(1): If an excavator contacts or damages an underground facility, the excavator shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-7(1)(a): immediately notify the appropriate operator and then proceed in a manner that is reasonably calculated to avoid further damage to the underground facility; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-7(1)(b): immediately call 911 if the excavation may result in an immediate risk to human life.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-7(2): Upon receipt of notice, the operator shall immediately examine the underground facility, and, if necessary, make repairs.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-7.5(1)(a): 54-8a-4; 54-8a-5.5; 54-8a-6 the excavator complies with Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-7.5(1)(b): the excavator demonstrates that the damage is the direct result of the operator's failure to locate its facility.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-7.5(2): (1) An excavator who damages a third-party operator's facility as described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-7.5(2)(a): shall pay for the costs of repairing the damaged facility; and

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-8(2)(b): 54-8a-4; (2)(a) an excavator who fails to provide notice of an excavation in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-9.5 Inspection of records.
------------------------------------------------------
The books and records of an association shall be open to inspection by its members during normal business hours upon 48 hours advance notice.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10 Installation of nonmetallic facilities.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Any operator installing a nonmetallic facility, such as a sewer, water, or fiber optic line, shall install the nonmetallic facility so that it can be located with standard underground facility detection devices or in a concrete conduit system.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5 Installation and location of sewer lateral cleanouts -- Records.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5(1)(a): An operator or person installing or replacing a sewer lateral cleanout beginning August 1, 2009 shall install or replace the sewer lateral cleanout in a manner so that the lateral can be located, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5(1)(a)(i): house sheets; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5(1)(a)(ii): electronic markers.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5(1)(b): An operator or person installing a sewer lateral cleanout shall notify the sewer operator of the sewer lateral cleanout location for record keeping purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5(2): Beginning on August 1, 2009, a sewer operator shall maintain records identifying where all new, replaced, or contractor-identified sewer lateral cleanouts are located within the sewer operator's jurisdiction.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5(3)(a): A sewer operator shall provide to an excavator information in the sewer operator's possession pertaining to a sewer lateral cleanout location within the sewer operator's jurisdiction.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-10.5(3)(b): The sewer operator shall provide the information within 48 hours of the excavator's request.


Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-11 Applicability of federal law.
------------------------------------------------------------
The following persons or entities are subject to the provisions of Title 49, Code of Federal Regulations, Part 198, Regulations for Grants to Aid State Pipeline Safety Programs, including those provisions relating to damage to underground facilities:Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-11(1): an operator, to the extent subject to the Pipeline Safety Improvement Act of 2002, 49 U.S.C. 60101 et seq.;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-11(2): an excavator; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-11(3): a person who operates an association.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-12(1)(a): The attorney general may bring an action in the district court located in the county in which the excavation is located to enforce this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-12(1)(b): The right of any person to bring a civil action for damage arising from an excavator's or operator's actions or conduct relating to underground facilities is not affected by:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-12(1)(b)(i): a proceeding commenced by the attorney general under this chapter; or

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-12(2): Any civil penalty imposed and collected under this chapter shall be deposited into the General Fund.


Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13 Underground Facilities Damage Dispute Board -- Arbitration -- Relationship with Public Service Commission.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(1): There is created within the commission the Underground Facilities Damage Dispute Board to arbitrate a dispute arising from:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(1)(a): an operator's or excavator's violation of this chapter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(1)(b): damage caused by excavation during an emergency.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(2): The board consists of five members appointed by the governor as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(2)(a): one member from a list of names provided to the governor by a group representing operators;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(2)(b): one member from a list of names provided to the governor by the Associated General Contractors;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(2)(c): one member from a list of names provided to the governor by Blue Stakes of Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(2)(d): one member from a list of names provided to the governor by the Utah Home Builders Association; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(2)(e): one member from the Division of Public Utilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(3)(a): A member of the board:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(3)(a)(i): shall be appointed for a three-year term; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(3)(a)(ii): may continue to serve until the member's successor takes office.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(3)(b): At the time of appointment, the governor shall stagger the terms of the members to ensure that approximately 1/3 of the members of the board are reappointed each year.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(3)(c): A vacancy in the board shall be filled:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(3)(c)(i): for the unexpired term; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(3)(c)(ii): in the same manner as the board member is initially appointed.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(3)(d): The board shall select an alternate for a specific board member to serve on a specific case if it becomes necessary to replace a member who has a conflict of interest because a dispute involves that member or that member's employer.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(4): Three members of the board constitute a quorum.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(5): The board may, upon agreement of the disputing parties, arbitrate a dispute regarding damages, not including personal injury damages, arising between:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(5)(a): an operator;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(5)(b): an excavator;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(5)(c): a property owner; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(5)(d): any other interested party.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(6): At least four members of the board shall be present and vote on an arbitration decision.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(7): Title 78B, Chapter 11, Utah Uniform Arbitration Act An arbitration before the board shall be consistent with
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(8): The prevailing party in an arbitration conducted under this section shall be awarded its costs and attorney fees in an amount determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(9): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 A member may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service, but may receive per diem and travel expenses in accordance with:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(9)(a): 63A-3-106 Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(9)(b): 63A-3-107 Section

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8a-13(10): The commission shall provide administrative support to the board.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 54 - Chapter 8b - Public Telecommunications Law
***************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1 Title.
------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Public Telecommunications Law."

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1 Legislative policy declarations.
----------------------------------------------------------------
The Legislature declares it is the policy of the state to:Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(1): 54-8b-11 endeavor to achieve the universal service objectives of the state as set forth in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(2): facilitate access to high quality, affordable public telecommunications services to all residents and businesses in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(3): encourage the development of competition as a means of providing wider customer choices for public telecommunications services throughout the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(4): allow flexible and reduced regulation for telecommunications corporations and public telecommunications services as competition develops;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(5): facilitate and promote the efficient development and deployment of an advanced telecommunications infrastructure, including networks with nondiscriminatory prices, terms, and conditions of interconnection;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(6): encourage competition by facilitating the sale of essential telecommunications facilities and services on a reasonably unbundled basis;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(7): seek to prevent prices for tariffed public telecommunications services or price-regulated services from subsidizing the competitive activities of regulated telecommunications corporations;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(8): encourage new technologies and modify regulatory policy to allow greater competition in the telecommunications industry;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(9): enhance the general welfare and encourage the growth of the economy of the state through increased competition in the telecommunications industry; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-1.1(10): endeavor to protect customers who do not have competitive choice.


Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2 Definitions.
------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(1): "Access line" means a circuit-switched connection, or the functional equivalent of a circuit-switched connection, from an end-user to the public switched network.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(2): (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(2)(a): "Aggregator" means any person or entity that:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(2)(a)(i): is not a telecommunications corporation;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(2)(a)(ii): in the ordinary course of its business makes operator assisted services available to the public or to customers and transient users of its business or property through an operator service provider; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(2)(a)(iii): receives from an operator service provider by contract, tariff, or otherwise, commissions or compensation for calls delivered from the aggregator's location to the operator service provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(2)(b): (2)(a) "Aggregator" may include any hotel, motel, hospital, educational institution, government agency, or coin or coinless telephone service provider so long as that entity qualifies under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3): "Basic residential service" means a local exchange service for a residential customer consisting of:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(a): a single line with access to the public switched network;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(b): touch-tone or the functional equivalent;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(c): local flat-rate unlimited usage, exclusive of extended area service;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(d): single-party service;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(e): a free phone number listing in directories received for free;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(f): access to operator services;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(g): access to directory assistance;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(h): access to lifeline and telephone relay assistance;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(i): access to 911 and E911 emergency services;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(j): access to long-distance carriers;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(k): access to toll limitations services;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(l): other services as may be determined by the commission; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(3)(m): no feature.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(4): "Certificate" means a certificate of public convenience and necessity issued by the commission authorizing a telecommunications corporation to provide specified public telecommunications services within a defined geographic service territory in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(5): 54-4a-1 "Division" means the Division of Public Utilities established in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(6): "Essential facility or service" means any portion, component, or function of the network or service offered by a provider of local exchange services:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(6)(a): that is necessary for a competitor to provide a public telecommunications service;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(6)(b): that cannot be reasonably duplicated; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(6)(c): for which there is no adequate economic alternative to the competitor in terms of quality, quantity, and price.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(7)(a): "Feature" means a custom calling service available from the central office switch, including call waiting, call forwarding, three-way calling, and similar services.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(7)(b): "Feature" does not include long distance calling.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(8): "Federal Telecommunications Act" means the Communications Act of 1934, as amended, and the Federal Telecommunications Act of 1996, Pub. L. No. 104-104, 110 Stat. 56.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(9): "Incumbent telephone corporation" means a telephone corporation, its successors or assigns, which, as of May 1, 1995, held a certificate to provide local exchange services in a defined geographic service territory in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(10): "Intrastate telecommunications service" means any public telecommunications service in which the information transmitted originates and terminates within the boundaries of this state.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(11): "Local exchange service" means the provision of telephone lines to customers with the associated transmission of two-way interactive, switched voice communication within the geographic area encompassing one or more local communities as described in maps, tariffs, or rate schedules filed with and approved by the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(12): "Mobile telecommunications service" means a mobile telecommunications service:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(12)(a): that is defined as a mobile telecommunications service in the Mobile Telecommunications Sourcing Act, 4 U.S.C. Sec. 124; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(12)(b): in which the information transmitted originates and terminates in one state.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(13): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(13)(a): "New public telecommunications service" means a service offered by a telecommunications corporation which that corporation has never offered before.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(13)(b): "New public telecommunications service" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(13)(b)(i): a tariff, price list, or competitive contract that involves a new method of pricing any existing public telecommunications service;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(13)(b)(ii): a package of public telecommunications services that includes an existing public telecommunications service; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(13)(b)(iii): a public telecommunications service that is a direct replacement for:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(13)(b)(iii)(A): a fully regulated service;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(13)(b)(iii)(B): an existing service offered pursuant to a tariff, price list, or competitive contract; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(13)(b)(iii)(C): an essential facility or an essential service.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(14): "Operator assisted services" means services which assist callers in the placement or charging of a telephone call, either through live intervention or automated intervention.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(15): "Operator service provider" means any person or entity that provides, for a fee to a caller, operator assisted services.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(16): 54-8b-2.3 "Price-regulated service" means any public telecommunications service governed by Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(17): "Public switched network" means the same as that term is defined in 47 C.F.R. Sec. 20.3.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(18): "Public telecommunications service" means the two-way transmission of signs, signals, writing, images, sounds, messages, data, or other information of any nature by wire, radio, lightwaves, or other electromagnetic means offered to the public generally.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(19): "Substantial compliance" with reference to a rule or order of the commission means satisfaction of all material obligations in a manner consistent with the rule or order.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(20): "Telecommunications corporation" means any corporation or person, and their lessees, trustees, receivers, or trustees appointed by any court, owning, controlling, operating, managing, or reselling a public telecommunications service.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(21): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(21)(a): "Total service long-run incremental cost" means the forward-looking incremental cost to a telecommunications corporation caused by providing the entire quantity of a public telecommunications service, network function, or group of public telecommunications services or network functions, by using forward-looking technology, reasonably available, without assuming relocation of existing plant and equipment.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2(21)(b): The "long-run" means a period of time long enough so that cost estimates are based on the assumption that all inputs are variable.


Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1 Competitive entry.
--------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(1): 54-4-25; (3)(c) Notwithstanding any provision of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(2): The commission shall issue a certificate to the applying telecommunications corporation if the commission determines that:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(2)(a): the applicant has sufficient technical, financial, and managerial resources and abilities to provide the public telecommunications services applied for; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(2)(b): the issuance of the certificate to the applicant is in the public interest.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(3): Title 63G, Chapter 4, Administrative Procedures Act; (1)
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(3)(a): Title 63G, Chapter 4, Administrative Procedures Act The commission shall process the application in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(3)(b): Each telecommunications corporation holding a certificate to provide public telecommunications service within the geographic area where an applicant is seeking to provide telecommunications service shall be provided  notice of the application and granted automatic status as an intervenor.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(3)(c): (1) An intervening incumbent telephone corporation serving fewer than 30,000 access lines in the state may petition the commission to exclude from an application filed pursuant to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(3)(d): The commission shall approve or deny the application under this section within 240 days after it is filed.  If the commission has not acted on an application within 240 days, the application is considered granted.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(4): If the commission issues a certificate to a competitive telecommunications corporation to provide local exchange services in a local exchange that has fewer than 5,000 lines and that is controlled by an incumbent telephone corporation with fewer than 30,000 access lines in the state, the commission shall impose an obligation upon the competitive telecommunications corporation to provide public telecommunications services to any customer or class of customers who requests service within the local exchange.  The competing telecommunications corporation's obligation to serve shall be no greater than that of the incumbent telephone corporation.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.1(5): An incumbent telephone corporation with fewer than 30,000 access lines in the state may not be required to become a carrier of intrastate toll services.


Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2 Interconnection.
------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(a)(i): The commission may require any telecommunications corporation to interconnect its essential facilities with another telecommunications corporation that provides public telecommunications services in the same, adjacent, or overlapping service territory.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(a)(ii): Interconnecting telecommunications corporations shall permit the mutual exchange of traffic between their networks without unreasonable blocking or other unreasonable restrictions on the flow of traffic.  In determining unreasonable blocking or unreasonable restrictions, the commission shall, among other things, take into account the necessity and time required for adapting the network to respond to significant changes in usage patterns.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(b)(i): Whenever the commission grants a certificate to one or more telecommunications corporations to provide public telecommunications services in the same or overlapping service territories, all telecommunications corporations providing public telecommunications services in the affected area shall have the right to interconnect with the essential facilities and to purchase the essential services of all other certificate holders operating in the same area on a nondiscriminatory and reasonably unbundled basis.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(b)(ii): Each telecommunications corporation shall permit access to and interconnection with its essential facilities and the purchase of its essential services on terms and conditions, including price, no less favorable than those the telecommunications corporation provides to itself and its affiliates.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(c): Nothing in this section shall prevent a telecommunications corporation from entering into nondiscriminatory agreements for interconnection with its essential facilities and the purchase and sale of essential services.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(d): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(d)(i): A telecommunications corporation shall file with the commission the prices, terms, and conditions of any agreement it makes for the interconnection of essential facilities or the purchase or sale of essential services.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(d)(ii): The agreement shall take effect 10 days after filing.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(d)(iii): Each telecommunications corporation shall allow any other telecommunications corporation to obtain interconnection with its essential facilities and to purchase essential services on prices, terms, and conditions no less favorable than those on file with the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(e): If there is a dispute over interconnection of essential facilities, the purchase and sale of essential services, or the planning or provisioning of facilities or unbundled elements, one or both of the disputing parties may bring the dispute to the commission, and the commission, by order, shall resolve the dispute on an expedited basis.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(1)(f): It is not a discriminatory pricing practice to vary prices to reflect genuine cost differences.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(2)(a): The commission shall adopt rules or issue an interim order which implements by December 31, 1996, the competitive provision of facilities-based intraLATA toll and local exchange services.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(2)(b): The rules or interim order shall address those issues the commission determines are essential for a competing telecommunications corporation to provide intraLATA toll and local exchange services and necessary to protect the public interest, including the interconnection with essential facilities and the purchase and sale of essential services of telecommunications corporations authorized to provide public telecommunications services in the same or overlapping service territories on a nondiscriminatory and reasonably unbundled basis.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(3)(a): By December 31, 1997, the commission shall adopt additional rules or issue a final order to implement the competitive provision of facilities-based intraLATA toll and local exchange services.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(3)(b): The rules or final order shall address other issues relating to:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(3)(b)(i): competition for intraLATA toll and local exchange services;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(3)(b)(ii): blocking, timing of provisioning of unbundled elements, and service quality standards for interconnecting carriers;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(3)(b)(iii): the transition to a competitive market; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(3)(b)(iv): the protection of the public interest.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(4): Nothing in this section shall require or prohibit the commission from ordering changes in dialing patterns for intraLATA toll services.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(5): (3) If the commission, by order, approves the application of a telecommunications corporation to provide public telecommunications services in all or part of the service territory certificated to an incumbent telephone corporation before the adoption of the rules or final order described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(5)(a): order the interconnection of essential facilities and the purchase and sale of the essential services of a telecommunications corporation with those of a competing telecommunications corporation on such terms and conditions and to the extent necessary to allow the competing telecommunications corporation to operate under authority granted by the commission; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-2.2(5)(b): address and resolve, by order, other issues necessary for the competitive provision of intraLATA toll and local exchange services.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3 Exemptions from requirements.
-----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(1): (1)(a); 54-1-3(2)(a); (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(1)(a): The commission, on its own initiative or in response to an application by a telecommunications corporation, a public agency, or a user of a public telecommunications service, may, after public notice and a hearing, issue an order exempting any telecommunications corporation or public telecommunications service from any requirement of this title, including any requirement or limitation relating to a telecommunication corporation's earnings, rate base, or pricing of public telecommunications services.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(1)(b): (1)(a); 54-1-3(2)(a); (1)(a) The commission may issue an order described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(1)(b)(i): 54-1-3(2)(a) the matter is not a proceeding described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(1)(b)(ii): (1)(a) a party to an application submitted under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(1)(b)(iii): no person opposes the request for informal adjudication before 10 business days after the day on which the party files the request.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(2): The commission shall specify in the order any requirements, terms, or conditions which may apply to any exemption.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(3): An exemption may be granted for the entire service territory of a telecommunications corporation or for a specific geographic area of the service territory.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(4): The commission may issue an order for an exemption only if it finds that:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(4)(a): the telecommunications corporation or service is subject to effective competition; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(4)(b): the exemption is in the public interest.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(5): In determining if the telecommunications corporation or service is subject to effective competition, the commission shall consider all relevant factors, which may include:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(5)(a): the extent to which competing telecommunications services are available from alternative telecommunications providers;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(5)(b): the ability of alternative telecommunications providers to offer competing telecommunications services that are functionally equivalent or substitutable and reasonably available at comparable prices, terms, quality, and conditions;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(5)(c): the market share of the telecommunications corporation for which an exemption is proposed;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(5)(d): the extent of economic or regulatory barriers to entry;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(5)(e): the impact of potential competition; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(5)(f): the type and degree of exemptions to this title that are proposed.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(6): In determining if the proposed exemption is in the public interest, the commission shall consider, in addition to other relevant factors, the impact the proposed exemption would have on captive customers of the telecommunications corporation.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(7)(a): The commission shall approve or deny any application for exemption under this section within 240 days, except that the commission may by order defer action for an additional 30-day period.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3(7)(b): If the commission has not acted on any application within the permitted time period, the application is considered granted.


Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3 Services that must be offered on a nondiscriminatory basis -- Public telecommunications to be cost-based -- Packaged services -- Quality of service standards.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(1)(a): As used in this section, "cost-based" means that the prices for the telecommunications services shall be established after taking into consideration the total service long-run incremental cost of providing the service.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(1)(b): The term "cost-based" does not prevent the establishment of prices:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(1)(b)(i): that promote the universal availability of service in the state; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(1)(b)(ii): that are offered by a telecommunications corporation for a public telecommunications service in a promotional offer, or market trial, or to meet competition.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(2)(a): a telecommunications corporation with more than 30,000 access lines in the state that provides a public telecommunications service may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(2)(a)(i): as to the pricing and provisioning of the public telecommunications service, make or grant any undue or unreasonable preference or advantage to any person, corporation, or locality; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(2)(a)(ii): in providing services that utilize the local exchange network:

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(2)(a)(ii)(B): subject any person, corporation, or locality to any undue or unreasonable prejudice or disadvantage;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(2)(b): public telecommunications services provided by a telecommunications corporation with more than 30,000 access lines in the state shall be nondiscriminatory, cost-based, and subject to resale as determined by the commission; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-3.3(2)(c): public telecommunications services may be packaged with other services, so long as they are also offered on a separate, unbundled basis.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-6 Prohibition on subsidization of telecommunications services.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
A telecommunications corporation providing intrastate public telecommunications services may not subsidize its intrastate telecommunications services which are exempted from regulation or offered pursuant to a price list or competitive contract under authority of this chapter with proceeds from its other intrastate telecommunications services not so exempted or made subject to a price list or competitive contract.  Similarly, proceeds from intrastate telecommunications services which are exempted from regulation or offered pursuant to a price list or competitive contract as authorized by this chapter may not subsidize other intrastate telecommunications services not so exempted or made subject to a price list or competitive contract.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-7 Continuous jurisdiction of commission -- Orders.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The commission shall retain continuous jurisdiction over every telecommunications corporation or public telecommunications service exempted under this chapter and may exercise any statutory grant of power pertaining thereto, including the power to revoke or modify any order approving an exemption from regulation.  The commission may, after notice and hearing, revoke or modify an order approving exemption, if after considering the factors in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-8 Antitrust and restraint of trade laws not affected by chapter.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Nothing in this chapter shall in any way preempt, modify, exempt, abrogate, or otherwise affect any right, cause of action, liability, duty, or obligation arising from any federal, state, or local law governing unfair business practices or antitrust, restraint of trade, or other anti-competitive activity.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-9 Commission's jurisdiction under other provisions of title not enlarged or reduced by chapter.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-9(1): Nothing in this chapter shall be construed to enlarge or reduce the commission's jurisdiction over the services and entities for which jurisdiction is provided or excluded by other provisions of this title.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-9(2): Nothing in this chapter shall be construed to enlarge the commission's jurisdiction over:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-9(2)(a): providers of:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-9(2)(a)(i): cellular or wireless telecommunications services; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-9(2)(a)(ii): the one-way transmission to subscribers of video programming and the subscriber interaction, if any, which is required for the selection of the video programming; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-9(2)(b): telecommunications companies classified as cooperatives.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-9(3): Nothing in this chapter shall diminish the commission's authority to regulate the quality of telecommunications services provided by telecommunications corporations.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-11 Establishing just and reasonable rates.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
In administering this title, the commission shall endeavor to make available high-quality, universal telecommunications services at just and reasonable rates for all classes of customers throughout this state.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13 Rules governing operator assisted services.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(1): The commission shall make rules to implement the following requirements pertaining to the provision of operator assisted services:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(1)(a): Rates, surcharges, terms, or conditions for operator assisted services shall be provided to customers upon request without charge.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(1)(b): A customer shall be made aware, prior to incurring any charges, of the identity of the operator service provider handling the operator assisted call by a form of signage placed on or near the telephone or by verbal identification by the operator service provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(1)(c): Any contract between an operator service provider and an aggregator shall contain language which assures that any person making a telephone call on any telephone owned or controlled by the aggregator or operator service provider can access:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(1)(c)(i): where technically feasible, any other operator service provider operating in the relevant geographic area; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(1)(c)(ii): the public safety emergency telephone numbers for the jurisdiction where the aggregator's telephone service is geographically located.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(1)(d): No operator service provider shall transfer a call to another operator service provider unless that transfer is accomplished at, and billed from, the call's place of origin.  If such a transfer is not technically possible, the operator service provider shall inform the caller that the call cannot be transferred as requested and that the caller should hang up and attempt to reach another operator service provider through the means provided by that other operator service provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(2): (2)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(2)(a): The Division of Public Utilities shall be responsible for enforcing any rule adopted by the commission under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(2)(b): If the Division of Public Utilities determines that any person, or any officer or employee of any person, is violating any rule adopted under this section, the division shall serve written notice upon the alleged violator which:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(2)(b)(i): specifies the violation;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(2)(b)(ii): alleges the facts constituting the violation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(2)(b)(iii): specifies the corrective action to be taken.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(2)(c): (2)(b) After serving notice as required in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(3)(a): Any person who violates any rule made under this section or fails to comply with any order issued pursuant to this section is subject to a penalty not to exceed $2,000 per violation.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(3)(b): In the case of a continuing violation, each day that the violation continues constitutes a separate and distinct offense.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-13(4): A penalty assessment under this section does not relieve the person assessed from civil liability for claims arising out of any act which was a violation of any rule under this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16 Public Service Commission authority to enforce interconnection service quality standards and interconnection agreements -- Grounds for filing complaint.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(1): For purposes of this section, "interconnection service quality standards" means specific, measurable criteria that shall be applied to a telecommunications corporation, including obligations pursuant to Section 251 of the Federal Telecommunications Act, regarding the telecommunications corporation's provision of or request for:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(1)(a): interconnection services;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(1)(b): services for resale;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(1)(c): unbundled network elements; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(1)(d): access to operations support systems that support those services and elements.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(2): To serve the public interest and to enable the development and growth of competition within the telecommunications market in the state, the commission shall, by order when considered necessary by the commission, enforce:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(2)(a): rules regarding interconnection service quality standards adopted by the commission under authority of this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(2)(b): a commission approved interconnection agreement pursuant to Sections 251 and 252 of the Federal Telecommunications Act; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(2)(c): a statement of generally available terms under Section 252(f) of the Federal Telecommunications Act.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(3): 54-8b-2.2(1)(e) An aggrieved party may file a complaint under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(3)(a): the terms of the commission's interconnection service quality rules;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(3)(b): the terms or conditions of an interconnection agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(3)(c): a statement of generally available terms; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(3)(d): a telecommunications corporations' obligations under the Federal Telecommunications Act.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(4): (3) In a proceeding described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(4)(a): the terms of the interconnection agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(4)(b): the commission's interconnection service quality rules;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(4)(c): the statement of generally available terms; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-16(4)(d): the telecommunications corporation's obligations pursuant to the Federal Telecommunications Act.


Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17 Procedures for enforcement of interconnection service quality -- Penalties for violation -- Funds collected.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1): 54-8b-2.2(1)(e) Proceedings under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1)(a): The complaint shall be served upon the defendant telecommunications corporation and filed with the commission.  A copy of the complaint shall also be served upon the Division of Public Utilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1)(b): An answer or other responsive pleading to the complaint shall be filed with the commission not more than 10 days after receipt of service of the complaint.  Copies of the answer or responsive pleading shall be served on the complainant and the Division of Public Utilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1)(c): A prehearing conference shall be held not later than 10 days after the complaint is filed.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1)(d): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1)(d)(i): The commission shall commence a hearing on the complaint not later than 25 days after the complaint is filed, unless the commission finds that extraordinary conditions exist that warrant postponing the hearing date, in which case the commission shall commence the hearing as soon as practicable.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1)(d)(ii): Parties shall be entitled to present evidence as provided by the commission's rules.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1)(e): The commission shall take final action on a complaint not more than 45 days after the complaint is filed unless:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1)(e)(i): the commission finds that extraordinary conditions exist that warrant extending final action, in which case the commission shall take final action as soon as practicable; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(1)(e)(ii): the parties agree to an extension of final action by the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(2): (3) The commission shall have the enforcement powers listed in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(2)(a): the telecommunications corporation has violated the terms of the commission's interconnection service quality rules;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(2)(b): the telecommunications corporation has breached its obligations under the provisions of the Federal Telecommunications Act;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(2)(c): either party to an approved interconnection agreement has violated the terms of the agreement; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(2)(d): either party has violated the terms of a statement of generally available terms.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(3): (2); 54-8b-2.2; 54-8b-16; 54-7-25; 54-7-25 If the commission makes any of the findings described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(3)(a): order the telecommunications corporation to:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(3)(a)(i): remedy the violation; and

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-17(3)(b): if considered appropriate by the commission, prescribe the specific actions that the telecommunications corporation must take to remedy its violation, including a time frame for compliance and the submission of a plan to prevent future violations;

Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18 Definitions -- Unauthorized change of telecommunications provider -- Unauthorized charges -- Procedures for verification -- Penalties -- Authority of commission.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(1): For purposes of this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(1)(a): "Agents" includes any person, firm, or corporation representing a telecommunications corporation for purposes of requesting a change in a subscriber's telecommunications provider, but does not include a local service provider when executing a request submitted by another service provider or its agents.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(1)(b): "Freeze" means a directive from a subscriber to retain the provider of public telecommunications services selected by the subscriber until the subscriber provides authorization for a change to another provider of public telecommunications services through any means by which a freeze is implemented.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(1)(c): "Small commercial subscriber" is a person or entity conducting a business, agriculture, or other enterprise in the state having less than five telecommunications lines.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(1)(d): "Subscriber" means a corporation, person, or government, or a person acting legally on behalf of a corporation, person, or government who has purchased public telecommunications services from a telecommunications corporation.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2): (2)(a); (e); (2); 13-26-4; 13-26-2; 13-26-8; 13-26-10; 13-26-11 No telecommunications corporation or its agents shall make any change or authorize a different telecommunications corporation to make any change in the provider of any public telecommunications service to a subscriber unless it complies, at a minimum, with Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(a): The telecommunications corporation or its agents shall, at a minimum, inform the subscriber of the nature, extent, and rates of the service being offered and any charges associated with the change.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(b): 13-26-4; 13-26-2; 13-26-8; 13-26-10; 13-26-11 Notwithstanding Section
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(c): For sales of residential service or small commercial subscriber service, the telecommunications corporation or its agents shall confirm that the subscriber is aware of any charges that the subscriber must pay associated with the change and that the subscriber authorizes the change of provider.  The subscriber's authorization to change the provider shall be confirmed by any one of the following methods:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(c)(i): obtaining the subscriber's written authorization;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(c)(ii): having the subscriber's oral authorization verified by an independent third party; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(c)(iii): any means provided by rule of the Federal Communications Commission or the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(d): If the subscriber is not an individual, an authorization shall be valid only if given by an authorized representative of the subscriber.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(e): 
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(e)(i): The written authorization to change the provider shall be signed by the subscriber and shall contain a clear, conspicuous, and unequivocal request by the subscriber for a change of telecommunications provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(e)(ii): A written authorization is not valid if it is presented to the subscriber for signature in connection with a sweepstakes, game of chance, or any other means prohibited by commission rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(2)(e)(iii): Nothing in this section shall be construed to prohibit any person from offering a premium, incentive, or a thing of value to another as consideration for authorizing a change of telecommunications service provider, provided that no element of chance or skill is associated with the offer of the premium, incentive, or thing of value or its receipt.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(3): The confirmation by a third-party verifier shall, at a minimum:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(3)(a): confirm the subscriber's identity with information unique to the customer, unless the customer refuses to provide identifying information, then that fact shall be noted;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(3)(b): confirm that the subscriber agrees to the requested change in telecommunications service providers; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(3)(c): confirm that the subscriber has the authority to select the provider as the provider of that service.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(4): A third-party verifier shall meet each of the following criteria:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(4)(a): any criteria for third-party verifiers set by the Federal Communications Commission;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(4)(b): not be directly or indirectly managed, controlled, directed, or owned wholly or in part:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(4)(b)(i): by the telecommunications corporation or its agents that seek to provide the telecommunications service or by any corporation, firm, or person who directly or indirectly manages, controls, directs, or owns more than 5% of the telecommunications corporation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(4)(b)(ii): by the marketing entity that seeks to market the telecommunications service or by any corporation, firm, or person who directly or indirectly manages, controls, directs, or owns more than 5% of the marketing entity;
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(4)(c): operate from facilities physically separated from:
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(4)(c)(i): those of the telecommunications corporation or its agents that seek to provide the subscriber's telecommunications service; or
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(4)(c)(ii): those of the marketing entity that seeks to market a telecommunications service to the subscriber; and
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(4)(d): not derive commissions or compensation based upon the number of change authorizations verified.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(5): A telecommunications corporation or its agents seeking to verify the change authorization shall connect the subscriber to the third-party verifier or arrange for the third-party verifier to call the subscriber to verify the change authorization.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(6): A third-party verifier that obtains the subscriber's oral verification regarding the change shall record that verification by obtaining appropriate verification data.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(7): (7)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(7)(a): The record verifying a subscriber's change of provider shall be available to the subscriber upon request.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(7)(b): Information obtained from the subscriber through verification may not be used for any other purpose.
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(7)(c): (7)(b) Any intentional unauthorized release of the information in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 54-8b-18(8): The third-party verification shall occur in the same language as that in which the change was solicited.
